-------------------------------------------------------------------------------- Page 95

## POSITION CONTROL REGISTER

![position control register]

```
REGISTER | BIT | MNEMONIC | FUNCTION |
|---|---|---|---|
PCR0 | 0 | MODE 1 | Position control mode |
PCR1 | 1 | MODE 2 | Velocity Control mode |
PCR2 | 2 | DIR | Direction of Movement |
PCR3 | 3 | INDEX SEL | Index signal active edge polarity selection |
PCR4 | 4 | HOME SEL | HOME Signal active edge polarity selection |
PCR5 | 5 | HOME | HOME Signal input status |
PCR6 | 6 | INDEX | INDEX Signal input status |
PCR7 | 7 | CLR FAULT | Clear fault flag |
PCR8 | 8 | SET LIMIT - | Set –LIMIT flag |
PCR9 | 9 | SET LIMIT + | Set +LIMIT flag |
PCR10 | 10 | LIMIT - | –Limit Signal Input Status |
PCR11 | 11 | LIMIT + | +Limit Signal Input Status |
PCR12 | 12 | CLR ABORT | Abort bit clearing function selection |
PCR13 | 13 | ABORT | Abort the current action |
PCR14 | 14 | STOP | Stop the motor immediately |
PCR15 | 15 | ENABLE | Enable the position controller |
```


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------- Page 96

## SECTION CONSOLIDATION

|                         | DATE    | TIME | TYPE  | COMMENT             |
| ----------------------- | ------- | ---- | ----- | ------------------- |
| 1.  INVESTIGATION BEGIN | 3-20-23 | 1036 | INIT  | CASE OPEN           |
